maṁgala-
( jāliharagacchīya siridēvasūriviraiyaṁ)
siripaumappahasāmicariya
maṁgalamāi - jiṇēsara - bhuya - daṁḍa - lulaṁta - kuṁtalā diṁtu ।
jiyamōha - hariya - sāmala - milaṁta - camara vva vilasaṁtā ॥9॥
niccaṁ niccala - cittā, jaṁ pattā saha nivāsaparamēṇa ।
laṁchaṇa- chalēṇa paumā, paumakaṁ namaha taṁ dēvaṁ ॥2॥
sō jayau saṁtināhō, appaḍicakkēhiṁ dōhi cakkēhiṁ ।
jassa nava - kuṁḍalēhiṁ va, mahi - mahilā gavvirī bhuvaṇē ॥3॥
jayau nava-mēha - sāmalataṇuṇō nēmissa ditti - pabbhārō ।
ājammadaddha-vammaha-dhūma - samūhu vva vilasaṁtō ॥4॥
nava-hattha-kāya-mahi-bhaya-haraṇaṁ kuvalaya- phuraṁta - varavannaṁ ।
gaya - rayamamōhanāmaṁ, namāmi dēvaṁ duhā pāsaṁ ॥ 5 ॥
mōttūṇa puraṁ purisā jassa susiddhaṁta - siddhamaṁtēṇa ।
pavisaṁti sivapuravarē, taṁ vīraṁ namaha jōiṁdaṁ ॥6॥
avasēsajiṇiṁdāṇa vi, sura-asura - nariṁda- caṁdabhālēsu
cūlāmaṇi vva kama - naha- kiraṇā vijayaṁtu dippaṁtā ||7||
uvasagga-vagga-takkaranivvāsaṇa - caṁḍa- ḍiṁḍima - samāṇā ।
jayau jiṇavayaṇa - niggaya - jōyaṇa - nihāriṇī vāṇī ॥8॥
bharahāisavvakhittēsu, jassa pasāēṇa niccamabhaviṁsu ।
hōhiṁti huṁti titthaṁkarā vi vijiyāya sō saṁghō ॥9॥
aṭṭhāvaya-vara-pavvaya - siharagayaṁ taha ya bhamaṇa - parimukkaṁ ॥
ahiṇava - ravimiva sirasā, gōyama - gaṇahāriṇaṁ namimō ॥10॥
jāyaṁ maha maṇagahaṇaṁ, saviyāsaṁ jēsimasamamāhappā |
guruṇō jayaṁtu tē maha, hiyayavasaṁtā vasaṁta vva ॥11॥

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
jēṇa vihiyāu dasa - disi kalimala - saṁharaṇa - sara - saricchāō ।
dasavaranijjuttīō, tassa namō bhaddabāhussa ॥12 ॥
jaṇa - maṇa - vaṇamaṁkuriyaṁ, jha tti suhāsāraṇīē vāṇīē ।
jēsiṁ niccaṁ tēsiṁ bhaddaṁ haribhaddasūrīṇaṁ ॥13॥
jassa gabhīrimajittō najjavi jalahī caēi khārataṁ ।
taṁ vivihagaṁthakārayamahivaṁdē hēmacaṁdapahuṁ ॥14॥
rayaṇāyara vva kaiṇō, annē vi jayaṁti jēsi rayaṇōhaṁ ।
giṇhiya suvaṇṇayārā, ghaḍati nava-navamalaṁkāraṁ ॥15॥
saguṇaṁ vi nigguṇaṁ vā, annaṁ savvaṁ sayā payāsaṁtā ।
appaṁ apayāsaṁtā suyaṇā naṁdaṁtu nayaṇasamā ॥ 16 ॥
ahavā
kō nāma nāmamittaṁ pi tāṇa suyaṇāṇa gihiē ? jēsiṁ ।
vivarīya sēharāṇaṁ phuraṁti dōsā vi guṇarūvā ॥17॥
jē navva-kavva - dōsaṁ nēva payaṁpaṁti jāṇamāṇā vi ।
tēsi mahāvērīṇaṁ, alaṁ pasaṁsāṇa suyaṇāṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
sayamēva dōsagāhī taha maha niṁdāiduguṇiucchāhō
payaḍissai maha dōsaṁ tattō niṁdāmi khalu piṇaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
alamēva vicchuyāṇaṁ, muhamēva ahīṇa taha ya maṁdassa ।
diṭṭhi cciya pisuṇāṇaṁ, savvaṁ savvassa bhayajaṇayaṁ ॥ 20 ॥
maṁtēṇa va cutrēṇa va, vicchuyapamuhāṇa havai paḍiyārō ।
dujjaṇajaṇapaḍiyārē, baṁbhā vi dhuvaṁ nirāraṁbhō ॥29॥
khaṁḍīkaō vi pajjāliō vi cunnīkaō vi cunnu vva
jīhāpalāiō vi hu jaṇēi dāhaṁ ahō ! pisuṇō ॥22॥
dō khaṁḍiō vi nikkīliō vi bhūmīē taha nihittō vi ।
niddala dhannanivahaṁ, bhamirō pisuṇō gharaṭṭu vva ॥23॥
guṇalavamavi saṁpāviya, tikkhā tucchā pahīṇacittā ya

=== devasuri1output-3-to-3.json ==========================
m
siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
sūi vva pisuṇajīhā, guṇamayamavi viṁdhaē sahasā ||24||
kaiyā vi kattha kahamavi, muhuttamittaṁ pi udayapattō vi ।
kēu vva ahō ! pisuṇō bhayāvahō bhuvaṇalōyāṇaṁ ॥25॥
sakkārasahassēhiṁ vi lavamavi pisuṇō na kijjaē suyaṇō ।
amayamaya aṁkapālīgaō vi kalusō cciya kalaṁkō ॥26॥
vihi-vilasiyāṇa khalabhāsiyāṇa taha mahilakūḍa - cariyāṇaṁ ।
maṇavaṁchiyāṇa pāraṁ vanai jai kaha vi savvannū ॥27॥
ēvaṁ kayatthiēṇaṁ, ahavā abbhatthiēṇa pisuṇēṇa
jō atthi majjha kavvē, sō dōsō tō kahēyavvō ॥28॥
jiṇanāha - namaṇa-saṁbhava - maṁgala-saṁhariya - vigdha - pabbhārō ।
siripaumappaha- cariyaṁ, kaya -acchariyaṁ bhaṇissāmi ॥ 29 ॥
jai vi jōisarāṇa vi, jiṇiṁda-cariyammi natthi sāmatthaṁ ।
taha vi balā vi payaṭṭara, maṁ jiṇapayapaṁkaē bhattī ॥30॥
jaha kēsimuttamāṇaṁ, saṁtē vi jiṇiṁda - biṁba- niuraṁbē ।
avaravara - biṁba - kāraṇavāvārō nipphalō nēya ॥31 ॥
taha paumappaha - pahuṇō, saṁtē vi hu avara - cariya - saṁdōhē ।
nahi nipphalō mamā vi hu imammi cariyammi vāvārō ॥32॥
risahēsarassa tērasa, bārasa saṁtissa nava ya nēmissa ।
dasa cēva pāsapahuṇō, sattāvīsaṁ ca vīrassa ॥33॥
avasēsajiṇiṁdāṇaṁ, kahiyā samayammi tinni tinni bhavā ।
iya paumappahacariyaṁ bhavatiyasahiyaṁ kahissāmi ॥34॥
suragirikaliyākaliō, nahayala - kajjalakavālasaṁjuttō
divu vva jaṁbūdīvō ihatthi lavaṇōyajalatillō ॥35॥
nahayalatamāla - taruṇō, āvālaṁ piva asēsamēhāṇaṁ ।
akkhayabhaṁḍāraṁ piva, lavaṇō uyahī taō bāhiṁ ॥ 36 ॥
bāhiṁ tassa ya dhāiyasaṁḍaṁ uddaṁḍaviviha-vaṇa-saṁḍaṁ ।

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
naga - nagara - sari-sarōvara - vāsajunaṁ atthi varadīvaṁ ॥37॥
tassēva majjhayārē mahāvidēhaṁ ti atthi varadīvaṁ ।
bahuvijaēhiṁ saṇāhaṁ, cakkaṁ piva cakkapāṇissa ॥38॥
jattha ya aṭhṭhāvīsaṁ, ukkōsā haṁti cakki - hali - hariṇō ।
battīsaṁ jiṇanāhā savvē caurō jahatrēṇaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
dupputtō viva mērū, taṁ kuṇai duhā ya tāyavihavaṁ va ।
puvvavidēhaṁ tattō, avaravidēhaṁ ca taṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 40 ॥
tattha ya puvvavidēhē, khaṁḍamivākhaṁḍalassa nayarīē ।
atthi sayā phalavacchaṁ, vacchaṁ nāmēṇa varavijayaṁ ॥41॥
tatthatthi hatthi - ghaṁṭā - ṭaṁkāra - raṇaṁta-gayaṇa - sīmaṁtā ।
pura- guṇa - gaṇa - nissīmā purī susīmā vigayasīmā ॥ 42 ॥
kōḍīsarabhavaṇōbbhiyakōḍipaḍāgāhiṁ sā purī mantrē ।
vihiyāvarapuravijayā, uddhabhuyā naccaē niccaṁ ॥ 43 ॥
sasikaṁtamaṇi - viṇimmiyapāsāyaparaṁparā vi rayaṇīē ||
amayamayasāraṇīhiṁ siṁcai gihakāṇaṇē jattha ॥44॥
maragaya - rayaṇa - viṇimmiya - tōraṇa- mittēṇa paulidārāṇi ।
phāliha - maṇisālāē, jattha jaṇō muṇaē kahakaha vi ॥45॥
jattha ya dāṇāivivihasaṁkalabaddhaṁ kaliūṇa niyasuyaṁ lacchiṁ
ummāhiu vva pattō agāhaparihāchalēṇuyahī ॥ 46॥
ummattakāmiṇīsuṁ, mārō daṁḍō vihārasiharēsu ।
kalahō gayasālāsuṁ, na uṇō tavvāsilōēsuṁ ॥47॥
bahudhanayajuyā alayaṁ, bahupurisuttamajuyā ya dāravaī ।
bahu jiē hu juyā amarāvaī pi mannē hasai ēsā ॥48॥
tīē purīē samiddhariddhiṁ niddhāriūṇa dharaṇiyalaṁ ।
dāriyarasāyalatalaṁ, mannē bhōgāvaī pattā ॥ 49॥
nāyavavasāyasahiō, mayarahiō puvvarāya abbhahiō ।
jittaṁ parājiō vi hu, rāyā aparājiō tattha ॥50॥

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
jassārinārisīmaṁtabahalasiṁdūrarēṇu - haraṇammi |
uvvahai samīrattaṁ aithirathōrō vi bhuyadaṁḍō ॥ 51 ॥
kuvvaṁti gaṁdha-baṁdhura-siṁdhura-ghaṁṭāṇa jassa ṭaṁkārā ।
pasaratā bhayabhiṁbhaladisigahaṇaparē disākariṇō ॥52॥
na sahai ēsō dōsaṁ maha uṇa gēhē timiṁgilagilattaṁ ।
iya saṁkiu vva jalahī jassa bhayā kaṁpaē niccaṁ ॥ 53 ॥
bhuvanabhavaṇaṁtarālē, arinārigalaṁtanittanīrēhiṁ ।
jassa payāvapaīvō, jalēi riu - salaha - khaya - kālō ॥54॥
caliyammi jammi sinā, dhūlī vi hu sūramaṁḍalaṁ sayalaṁ
paḍihayatēyappasaraṁ karēi kiṁ vannimō tassa ? ॥ 55 ॥
bhūvāla- bhāla-tilayāvalīhiṁ ciṁcaiyacaraṇatāmarasō ।
niravajjaṁ niyarajjaṁ, paripālaṁtō gamai kālaṁ ॥56॥
aṁgulimuddāvajjiyasahāvasuumārapāṇikamalēhiṁ ।
vāravilayāhiṁ saṇiyaṁ saṁvāhijjaṁtakamakamalō ॥57॥
atthāṇa suhāsīṇō, ciṭṭhai avarājiō nivō jāva ।
tā māgahēṇa paḍhiyaṁ samarāraṁbhābhihāṇēṇa ॥ 58 ॥ juyalaṁ
ēsō kiṁsuya - kanniyāra - kaliyā kōsuṁbharattaṁbarō ।
sāṇaṁdaṁ kalakaṁṭhikaṁṭha kuharāgijjaṁtagēyajhuṇī ।
ārūḍhō malayānilaṁ mayagalaṁ rōlaṁbarōlāulaṁ ।
rammārāmasiriṁ vivāhiumaṇō pattō vasaṁtō varō ॥59॥
vijayāya tujjha naravara ! vasaṁtasamayassa havau āraṁbhō ।
parivaḍḍhisāraṁbhō tihuyaṇavijayammi mayaṇassa ॥60॥
duiēṇa baṁdiviṁdāraēṇa naranāhahiyayaullāsaṁ ।
jaṇayaṁtēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, vijayāraṁbhābhihāṇēṇa ॥ 61॥
ihiṁ māṇiṇimāṇasēladalaṇē niddabhadaṁbhōliṇō ।
hēmaṁtappasaratakittikayalīduddatadaṁtābalō ॥

kakkōlī - lavalī - lavaṁga-tagarīnippaṭṭanaṭṭāvayā ।
tē vāyaṁti samīraṇā virahiṇī niddakkhiṇā dakkhiṇā ॥ 62 ॥
jayamavi samīravīrā vasē kuṇaṁtā aṇaṁga āṇāē ।
tuha suha - nivahullāsaṁ, kuṇaṁtu mahusamaya - maha - mahiyā ॥ 63 ॥
tēsiṁ vasaṁtavaṇṇaṇatakkhaṇasaṁjāyapulaya - pabbhārō ।
viyarai sa camakkārō, rāyā vi hu vihavasaṁbhāraṁ ॥64॥
ujjāṇapālaēṇa vi vasaṁtapālēṇa namiya vittaṁ ।
avainō mahusamaō, samaō pahu ! tujjha kīlāē ॥ 65 ॥
phulliya - vallī - mallī - hallīsaya - nivahamajjhayārammi ।
aliula-ravēhiṁ gāyai, mahusamaō tujjha guṇanivahaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
dāūṇa pāritōsiyāṇaṁ rāyā vasaṁtapālassa ।
caliō kāṇaṇalacchiṁ picchiukāmō saparivārō ॥67॥
taṁbakka - bukka - ḍhakkā - kāhala - kaṁsālagahirasaddēhiṁ ।
tharahariyasāyarajalō, sāyarabaṁdiyaṇathuvvaṁtō ||68 ||juyalaṁ ॥
jaṁpāṇa - jāṇa - vāhaṇa - sukkhāsaṇa - nara - vimāṇa - raha - nivahē ।
sijjāvālaya - siṁdhura- vahilla - varavāhalaṁghaṇiyā ॥ 69 ॥
āruhiya saha piyāhiṁ, baṁdhura - siṁgāra - bhāsura - sarīrō ।
sāmaṁta maṁti- pamuhō, saha ratnā vaccaē lōō ॥70॥
sīmaṁtiṇī samūhā, kaḍakkhavikkhēvaamaya laharīhiṁ ।
kāṇaṇatilayaṁ tilayaṁ maṁjariyaṁ jhatti kuvvaṁti ॥ 71 ॥
muha. kamalaniggaēṇaṁ, kariti vāruṇirasēṇa taruṇīō ।
ullasiyaphullanivahaṁ, mahuyaramālāulaṁ baulaṁ ॥72॥
virahiyadumasamavāyaṁ, karēi aṁkūraniyaradaṁturiyaṁ ।
kamaṇīyakāmiṇīyaṇagaō suhā mahuragēyaravō ॥73॥
ramaṇīya - ramaṇi - nivahā, kuṇaṁti raṇajhuṇiramaṁjumaṁjīrā ।
ullasiyapallavilliṁ, kaṁkilliṁ pāyaghāēhi ॥74 ||

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
kuruvayatarunikuraṁbaṁ, karaṁti ghaṇasihiṇa - vibbhamā sahasā ।
pariraṁbhiyasāraṁbha aṁkuriyaṁ jāyapulayaṁ va ॥ 75 ॥
iya ēvaṁvihavaiyaraphulliyavaṇarāirāiyaṁ rammaṁ ।
ārāmaṁ saṁpattō, iṁdiṁdirasuṁdaraṁ rāyā ॥ 76 ॥
jalakēli - kusuma - nicayāvacāyapamuhāhiṁ vivihalīlāhiṁ ।
saṁtēuraparivārō ārāmē ramai sō tattha ॥77॥
aliulakuvalaya-kajjala-tamāla - tamasāmalāō gayaṇāō ।
avayaramāṇaṁ kuṁḍala - kirīḍavarahāradippataṁ ॥78॥
caudaṁta- daṁti-kaṁdhara- mārūḍhaṁ surasamūhapariyariyaṁ ।
karavilasirasayadhāraṁ, puraṁdaraṁ picchaē rāyā ॥79॥
vipphāriyaniyanittō, sahassanittaṁ niittu naranāhō ।
ciṁtai imassa rūvaṁ, abhirūvaṁ tihuyaṇē sayalē ॥80॥
mantrē dhannō ahayaṁ, kāṇaṇagamaṇaṁ tahēva maha sahalaṁ ।
niyadittivijiyaakkō, sakkō sayamēva jaṁ diṭṭhō ॥81॥
hariparipēsiyasiṁdhuranāhēṇaṁ picchirammi naranāhō ।
vihiyaṁ payāhiṇātigamā rāmāsavrasēlassa ॥ 82 ॥
ōyariyasiṁdhurāō, baṁdhurarōmaṁca aṁciyasarī ।
girisiharakāṇaṇatthaṁ, muṇināhaṁ namai suranāhō ॥83॥
hari - hariṇagamēsāī, tāḍaṁtā duduhīō kusumāṇi ।
varisaṁtā varamuṇiṇō kēvalimahimaṁ pakuvvaṁti ॥84॥
viyasiyanittō tattō, saha nayarijaṇēṇa udayasēlaṁ va ।
udayābhimuharavī viva, taṁ nagamāruhai naranāhō ॥ 85 ॥
kaṇayamayapaṁkayagayaṁ, paccakkhaṁ - mukkha sukkha - nivahaṁ ca ।
rāgāidamaṇadakkhaṁ ariṁdamaṁ nāma muṇināhaṁ ॥86॥
picchai taō namaṁsai sō rāyā rāya - raṁkasamacittaṁ ।
rūvēṇa uvasamēṇa ya, jiyamāraṁ ciṁtaē tattō ॥87॥

=== devasuri1output-8-to-8.json ==========================
siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
mantrē kalaṁkamaliṇaṁ appāṇaṁ ciṁtiūṇa hariṇakō ।
ēsō tavaṁ pavannō, kalaṁkapaṁkāvahāratthaṁ ॥88॥
kannābhigamaṇadūsaṇaharaṇatthaṁ vā tavēi kiṁ tavaṇō ? |
ahavā ēsa jayaṁtō, tava tavaṁ sāvapabbhaṭṭhō ॥89॥
kiṁ tavai ēsa mārō, kumāravijayāya niccamujjuttō ।
nāmaṁ pi hu niṭṭhaviḍaṁ, kāmassa imō kumārō vā ॥90॥
sura-asurakhayara kinnara - naridavaṁdēhaṁ sāyaraṁ muṇiṇō ।
vaṁdijjaṁtē jaṁ taṁ tavassa mahimāē mahamahiyaṁ ॥ 91 ॥
saggāpavagganavapurapavisiranaravisaramaṁgaluggārā ।
duhasēlakulisadhārā, dhammakā patthuyā muṇiṇā ॥ 92 ॥
iha dulahō narajammō, dulahā sukulubbhavāya sāmaggī ।
dulahō jiṇiṁda - dhammō pamāyacāō tahā dulahō ॥93॥
saṁpattaṁ sāmaggiṁ jō hārai visamavisayavisagiddhō ।
sō mānasa - sarasalilaṁ, muṁcai māyaṇhiyā kajjē ॥94॥
visayāmisalavagiddhō sivasammakaraṁ pi cayai jō dhammaṁ ।
gaṁdhavvanayarakajjē, sō dhuvamamarāva cayai ॥95॥
vajjittu tō pamāyaṁ visayasuhāsaṁgaraṁgamujjhittā ।
kayasammē jiṇadhammē, sammaṁ ujjamaha ājammaṁ ॥ 96 ॥
jōyaṇasahassasōlasasalilasihāsēharō vi jalarāsī ।
jaṁ na virillai vasuhaṁ, taṁ jāṇasu dhammamāhappaṁ ॥97॥
hāla - hari - nariṁda- caṁdā, asuriṁda- khayara - nāgiṁdā |
savvē vi jiṇavariṁdā havaṁti dhammappasāēṇaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
kiṁ payaḍaha payasēvaṁ nariṁda - gōviṁda-khaṁda - iṁdāṇaṁ ? ॥
ikkaṁ karēha dhammaṁ, havaṁti jaṁ tē vi dhammēṇaṁ ॥ 99 ॥
sō vi hu cauppayārō, caugai - bhava- tikkha - dukkhasaṁhārō ।
bhaṇiō jiṇēhiṁ dāṇaṁ, sīlaṁ tava - bhāvaṇā cēva ॥100॥

kiṁtu ahaṁ ajjēva ya, rajassalā samayavihiya navavasaṇā ।
jai kahavi havai gabbhō, tō haṁ kaha hōmi tuha virahē ? ||607॥
paumā gayachaumā vi hu, tō maṁ nivvāsihī dhuvaṁ pacchā ।
kiṁ na suyaṁ nāha ! taē, sāsūṇa vahūhiṁ saha vēraṁ ॥ 608 ||
sō āha bhīru ! muddārayaṇaṁ giṇhēsu maha ahiṇāṇaṁ ।
appasa niyayaṁ hāraṁ, maha maṇakayasōkkhasaṁbhāraṁ ||609 ॥
iya jaṁpiya niyamappiya, muddārayaṇaṁ imīi taha hāraṁ ।

ittō ya caviya taiyā, dēvanivāsāu divvajōēṇaṁ ।
,
uyarammi tīē uttamasurajīvō kō vi avayariō ॥611॥
aha saha vaḍḍhai gabbhō mayaṁkalēhāē ajasapaṁkēṇaṁ ।
davaṇa imaṁ paumā, kuviyā taṁ pai payaṁpēi ॥ 612 ॥

kuladhammō amha imō, jīviyadāṇaṁ pamuttūṇaṁ ॥ 708 ॥
ēkkaṁ kijjai kajjaṁ, vahaṇijjāṇaṁ taō payaṁpēha ।
iṭṭhē kiṁci vi kajjaṁ, baṁdigaṇō ciṁtaē tattō ॥ 709 ॥
kuladhammē kulisasayaṁ, nivaḍau ēyassa jammi jīvāṇaṁ ।
kaṁpirataṇūṇa jīyaṁ, hariūṇaṁ dijjaē avaraṁ ॥ 710 ॥
jō niyajīviyakajjē, caēi amarīvaīē rajjaṁ pi ।
kaha tavvighāyapāvō, phiṭṭai avarēhiṁ dāṇēhiṁ ॥ 711 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca
mērugirikaṇayadāṇaṁ, dhannāṇaṁ dēu kōḍirāsīō ।
ēkkaṁ vahēi jīvā, na chuṭṭaē tēṇa dāṇēṇa ॥ 712 ॥
ēvaṁ viciṁtayaṁtō bhaṇijjamāṇā vi tēṇa puṇaruttaṁ ।
baṁdigaṇō bhīyamaṇō na kiṁ pi paḍijaṁpiō tassa ॥71 3 ॥
jaṁpai mayaṁkalēhā, ahayaṁ patthēmi bhāya ! kajjamimaṁ ।
paḍhamaṁ ciya maṁ mārasu, puraō caṁḍīi ēyāē ॥714॥
sō āha kō visēsō, maraṇē patthāvapuvvaō vihiē ? ।
sā āha maē paḍhamaṁ, mārijjaṁtē na picchissaṁ ॥715 ॥
acchīhiṁ picchiuṁ pi hu, sōuṁ savaṇēhiṁ akkhamā ahayaṁ
jīva tō paḍhamaṁ marēmi jai tō bhavē bhavvaṁ ॥ 716 ॥
suṁdarabuddhī suṁdaranāmā tattō payaṁpaē jāmi ! ।
taṁ gaccha maē mukkā, jīsē ēyārisā buddhī ॥717॥
sā āha bhāya ! nāhaṁ, ēkkā gacchāmi kaha va jīvaṁtī ।
pacchā mārijjaṁtē, muttuṁ savvē imē baṁdē ॥718 ।।

chēēṇa tēṇa ratnā, purassa īsāṇakōṇasamma ।
nimmāviya maṇibhavaṇaṁ, ēsā mukkā tahiṁ kannā ॥1113॥
sā nārī parivārā, kahamavi maṇibhavaṇasiharamārūḍhā ।
.
picchēi samarasīhaṁ, pavisaṁtaṁ nayaramajjhammi ॥ 1114 ॥
mannai maṇammi ēsā, imassa narasēharassa amayamayā ।
kā vi navā taṇulacchī, gaī vi avarā navā kā vi ॥1115 ॥
mantrē narō na ēsō, kiṁ puṇa amhārisāṇa suhīyāṇa ।

jammasayarammapimmō, tattō maha kō vi baṁdhavō ēsō ।

jayalacchīmāhavaṁtā, vīrā varisaṁti saravisaraṁ ॥ 1212 ॥
gayaputrāṇa narāṇa va, maṇōrahā rahiyacakkavaṭṭīhiṁ ।
anōnnaṁ tēhi sarā, addhapahē cēva nicchinnā ॥ 1213 ॥
viyaraṁtā saravisaraṁ, duguṇaṁ duguṇaṁ ca dō vi tavvēlaṁ ।
picchiya surēhiṁ diṭṭhā, ahiṇavaahimanusāricchā ॥1214 ॥
niravikkhaṁ naracaṁdō, ayāṇamāṇō haṇēi niyataṇayaṁ ।
sāvikkhaṁ niya jaṇayaṁ, jāṇatō pahaṇaē kumarō ॥1215 ॥
naracaṁdanariṁdas ya, jahatthanāmēṇa samarasīhēṇa ।
kō daṁḍacaṁḍadaṁḍō, vikkhaṁḍiō kharakhurappēṇa ॥1216॥
jaṁ jaṁ rāyā taiyā, giṇhai bāṇāsaṇaṁ ca sāmarisō ।
taṁ taṁ kumarō khaṁḍai, payaṁḍabāṇēhiṁ jā vīsaṁ ॥1217॥
khaṇamittēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ, cchinnaṁ chattaṁ paḍāiyā chinnā ।
chinnō ya rahō saṁgaramaṇōharō tassa naravaiṇō ॥1218॥
ciṁtai cittē rāyā, (aha) ahayamimēṇa pariyaravikō ।
ullūriya navapallavalavō vva rukkhō kaō sahasā ॥1219 ॥

paḍiō nivapayapuraō, vāyai rāyaṁ imaṁ gahiuṁ ॥ 1220 ॥

rajjaṁ baṁdhaṇarajjū, dēhaṁ dahaṇō dhaṇaṁ pi nighaṇaṁ va ।
mārō viva parivārō, tīē viṇā majjha paḍihāi ॥ 1412 ॥
jīē nisāē diṭṭhā, jīē picchissamahava tē dō ।
sahalā gaṇēmi sēsō, palālasarisō imō jammō ॥1413 ॥
jō kō'vi kanayaṁ taṁ puṇaravi dāvēi ēkkavēlaṁ pi ।
vēlaṁ ājammaṁtaṁ, vahēmi suyaṇassa tassāhaṁ ॥1 41 4।।
taṁ muṇiya garuyaciṁtā jarajajjariyaṁ va avaradīvammi ।
ōsahigavēsaṇamaṇō, saṁpattō ōsahīnāhō ॥1415 ॥
paḍupaḍaha-bhēri - jhallari - sudhīra-gaṁbhīra - tūra - ārāvō !

ēva kathayitu । sa prāha- mūrkha ! ēkānnaviṁśaṁ śataṁ yōjanānāṁ sa dēśō vartattē, na

atha vaiśvānarasyaiva kanīyasā sōdarēṇa mahāśailanāmmrā kumāramitrēṇa karṇābhyarṇamupētya
prōcē - kumāra ! yadi tavāpya yamasthānasamarthanagarvaparvatō durātmā sabhāyāṁ ajñānaṁ
prakāśayāmāsa tarhi kiṁ jīvītavyēna ? kiṁ vā anēna parirakṣitēna ? kiṁ vā tayā

“kumāra ! pūrvapuruṣairāghāṭaghaṭitaśilāvinyāsapūrvakaṁ yōjanānāmasmin pa

bruvāṇē yadā rājā dūrē na bhavati tadā vaiśvānararūpa ēva sampanna ēkainaiva nistriṁśa
prahārēṇa tau dūta - rājānau caṇḍacaṇḍālādapyadhikakarmā nijaghāna । atha tadasambhāvyaṁ
kumārakamavalōkya sakalamāsthānaṁ cukṣōbha । samajaniṣṭasakalē'pi tatra nagarē mahān
kōlāhalaḥ । taṁ ca tumulamākarṇya kumārajananī nandādēvī vatsa ! kimidaṁ bhavatā
mlēcchairapya bhāṣaṇīyama śrōtavyamacintanīyaṁ karmasamācaritam ? nivartasva karavālaṁ
pratyākārē nikṣipasva, kuruṣva jananī jalpitamiti jalpantī kumārapārśvamagamat ।
-----
atha vaiśvānarēṇābhihitaḥ kumāraḥ । paśya madīyāṁ śaktiṁ yadēkēnaiva nistriṁśa
prahārēṇa dvāvapi dūta - rājānāvupasaṁhr̥tau bhavatā; ētāmapi pātakinī vibruvāṇāṁ māsma
titikṣēthāḥ, yā kila bhavantamapi tējasvicakavartinaṁ pāpakarmāṇamabhidhattē ।
ityātradyabhidadhatā tēna pāpamitrēṇa punastarāmāviṣṭō mutkalakuntalakalāpaḥ
pratyakṣamahāpiśācastasyā api nalinīnālalīlāyitēnaiva nistriṁśēna śirō lulāva |
athānilasahitamivadāvānalaṁ tamasādhyamālōkya sambhūya sarvē'pi sāmantādayō rājalōkā
yaṣṭi-muṣṭi-lēṣṭu-laguḍa - pāṣṇipramukhaistaṁ kuṭṭayitvā jarjaraprāyaṁ kr̥tvā babandhurmahatā

kapāṭasampuṭaṁ pidhāya
pidhāya dhārayāmāsuḥ । atha sahasradīdhitāvastamupēyuṣi
astōkaśōkāndhakāragrastē ca sarvasminnapi purī lōkē kr̥tē ca dūtarājarājñīnāmauva
dēhikē karmaṇi vilapya vilapya viśrāntē ca sakala śuddhāntē prāptē ca niśīthasamayē
sa durātmā tēnaiva pāpamitrēṇa saha paryālōcya bandhaprabandhaṁ trōṭayitvā kapāṭasampuṭaṁ
śanairudghāṭya puralōkaṁ pratijvalita iva pratigr̥haṁ pratipāṭakaṁ vahni prakṣipya kr̥takr̥tya
iva bāṇāsaṇa - tūṇāhastō nagarānniragacchat । gacchaṁśca kiyatā kālēna
kuśasthalanāmānaṁ grāmaṁ samprāptaḥ । tat parisara ēva tr̥ṣārtō jalapānārthamēkamagā

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
1
yadi svapratijñāṁ smarasi tadā sāmprataṁ mamētasyā api sparśa viṣayī kuruṣva ।
itthaṁ tēna prēritaḥ sa sarōmbhasi praviśya grahagr̥hīta iva mattaivāndha iva tayā saha
kiñcidālāpamātraṁ vidhāya sparśasukhalālasaḥ parirambhamārabhatē sma । sā'pi tathaiva tēna
sparśanēna prōtsāhitā tamabhirāmaṁ vigrahamālōkya jātakautukā gāḍhamāśliṣat ।
athadaivavaśa tastasyāḥ kuraṅgikābhidhānāyāḥ kuraṅgō nāma mlēcchādhipatirnija
prēyasīṁ saraḥ prāptāṁ vijñāya jalakēlayē hastanyastakārmukabhallīkaḥ saraḥ salilamagacchat ।
taṁ tathā'valōkya sañjāta kōpātirēkaḥ kārmukamārōpya bhallīṁ sandhāya sākṣēpamēnamāhmasta
arē ! pāpa ! māmakīnāṁ prāṇapriyāmabhiramamāṇō dhruvaṁkīnāśaniśāntagamanamabhilaṣasi --
iti vibruvāṇēna tēna saha sa rājaputrō nijapāpamitrābhyāṁ vaiśvānaramahāśailābhyāmutsāhitō
durddharaṁ samaramakārṣīt । tāvanyōnyabhallīghātanihatau sarastīrē prāṇairjhagiti tatyajātē ।
taiḥ pāpamitrai stribhirapi tau ṣaṣṭhanarakapr̥thivyāṁ ninyātē । tatra gurumudagaragadādipraharaṇaiḥ
parasparaṁ praharantau kṣētrasvabhāvasamutthaśītavēdanāta nityamatyavāvahatāṁ dvāviṁśati
sāgaramānamāyuḥ । tatō'pyuddhartitaḥ sa saṁsārijīvaḥ pāpamitrasamanvitō matsya - sarpa-
siṁha śyēnādibhavāntarē kr̥tvā duḥsahaduḥkhanivahamanubhavannēkaikasyāṁ narakapr̥thivyāṁ dvidvirabhrāmyata
I atha nirjīrṇaprāyēṣu pūrvāpārjitapāpēṣu samutpannō bahiraṅganagaya bāṇārasyāṁ
ghanarathamahīnāthapaṭṭadēvyāḥ prabhāvatyāḥ kukṣau kukṣirōhaṇabhūmiratnāyamānō mahāpadmō nāma
kumāraḥ । tasya tadā rāgakēsarisutaḥ sāgaraka nāma antaraṅgamitramajaniṣṭa sa
sākṣiṇamupādhyāyaṁ kr̥tvā kalākalāpaṁ nikhilamagrahīt ।
itaśca śubhōdayamahārājaputrō nijacārutā garbhasambhūtaḥ sarvaguṇasampūrṇastasya
kumārasya mitramabhūd vicakṣaṇō nāma । tēna vicakṣaṇēna vimalamāna sapurādhipatēḥ
kalmaṣakṣayanr̥pasya duhitā sundaratāgarbhasambhūtā buddhirnāma kanyakā svayaṁvarāyātā
janakādēśatō mahōtsavapūrvakaṁ pariṇinyē । sā śatapatranētrānijaprēyasinitāntamanuraktā
tasyaiva pārśvē ciraṁ tasthau । atha raṇaraṇakēna gr̥hītaḥ kalmaṣakṣayanr̥pativimarśanāmānaṁ
svaputraṁ nijaduhitr̥vārtā pracchanāya prāhiṇōt । sō'pi vicakṣaṇasamīpa ēva jāmi
snēhamōhitaḥ prabhūtakālaṁ tasthau । kālakramēṇa budhdē : prakarṣō nāma sarvalakṣaṇaḥ sutaḥ
saṁjajñē । atha mahāpadmavicakṣaṇau vadanakōṭaraṁ nāma kānanaṁ kadācid gatavantau । antaḥ

vimarśaḥ prāha tarhi tat kaṭakaṁ sāmprataṁ kutra vartatē ? 'mithyābhimānēna '
cintitam - nūnaṁ hērikāvētau ataēva samūlāṁ sarva śuddhiṁ pr̥cchataḥ । tataḥ prōktam-
sāmprataṁ dēvaḥ sasainyastāmasacittē nagarē śrūyatē । atha tathā āpr̥cchya tau bhōjanādi
tatra kr̥tvā punaragrē pratasthātē । gacchaṁśca vimarśa : prakarṣaṁ pratyāha vatsa ! labdhā
kiyatī tāvad rasanāyā' mūlaśuddhiḥ । paripūrṇā punavirṣayābhilāṣaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā
jñāsyāmaḥ । kramēṇa prāptau tāmasacittē । tatra tābhyāṁ pravēśaṁ kurvāṇābhyāṁ tatraiva
praviśan dr̥ṣṭō 'dainyā'kraṁndarōdanādi katipayapuruṣaparivāritō dhūmasamūhasamānadēhaḥ
śōkanāmā pratijāgarukaḥ pāḍīrikaḥ । sa pr̥ṣṭastābhyām “bhadra ! kō'tra rājā ?
tēnābhihitam mahāmōhanr̥patēstanayō rāgakēsariṇō'nujaḥ sugr̥hītanāmadhēyō 'dvēṣagajēndrō ṁ
nāma, sō'pi santōṣasyōpari sabalavāhanaścalitō vartatē, sāmprataṁ punastat, kaṭakaṁ
'cittavr̥tti' mahāṭavyāṁ pramattatā' nadyāstīrē sarvamapyāyāsitamāstē, durātmanaḥ santōṣasyātra
nagarē ghāṭīṁ pātitāṁ । śrutvā svayaṁ dēvēnāhaṁ punaratra viśuddhikaraṇāya prēritō'smi ।
atha tau tadapi puraṁ sakalamapi nirīkṣya prāptau kramēṇa cittavr̥tti' mahāṭavyāṁ ।
dr̥ṣṭā tatra tābhyāṁ ninādipayaḥpūraduṣprēkṣā apara pārāvāragāminī 'pramattatā' nāma
mahāvāhinī । avalōkitaṁ tasyāḥ pulinē samāvāsitaṁ kr̥tamahākalakalaṁ hēti
nivahadūrālōkaṁ saṅkhyātītasubhaṭakōṭisaṅkīrṇa mōharājasya sainyam । nirūpitastatra
nabhōbhāgamavarundhānaḥ trilōkīlōkasantrā samādadhānō dūrādēva vilōkyamānaścittavikṣēpō
nāma mahāmaṇḍapaḥ । pratyakṣīkr̥tastēna mahāmaṁḍalēśvaranikaraparivāritastr̥ṣṇā
vēdikāsthitaviparyayābhidhānasiṁhāsanādhyāsīnō mahābhairavīmavidyāṁ nāma gātrayaṣṭiṁ dadhānaḥ,
kadāgrahanivaharūpakacanicayanirmitaṁ kūrcaṁ muhurmuhuḥ parāmr̥śan, rajastamōrūpābhyāṁ
nayanābhyāṁ jagattrayamapi kaṭākṣayan, tamālatamastōmaśyāmacchāyakāyō, mamētyadhyavasāyātmā,
nirjitasakalasarā asurēndraḥ śrīmanmahāmōhanarēndraḥ । taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā vimarśaprakarṣāvapi
nirjitasakalasurāasurēndraḥ
kṣubhitāviva dūrē tasthivāṁsau, na punarantarāsthānamaṇḍapamavikṣātām । prakarṣaḥ prāha
māma ! mama kathaya pratyēkamētēṣāṁ mahāmōhamaṇḍalēśvarāṇāṁ svarūpam ।
-
atha 'vimarśō'pi vimr̥śya prāha āyuṣman ! iyaṁ tāvanmōharājasya
vāmapārśvē niṣaṇṇā kuṭṭinī samānasthūlataraśarīrā 'mahāmūḍhatā nāma paṭṭadēvī । ayaṁ
punarasya rājñaḥ sarvavyāpārādhikārī nikaṭasthita ēvamithyābhinivēśasiṁhāsaṇāsīnō

sō jaṁpai hē lōē haṁhō nivamitta ! majjha vayaṇēṇaṁ ।
āgacchasuṁ jaṁ rāyā ciṭṭhai tuha virahasaṁtattō ॥ 626॥
aṁjiyanayaṇō puvvaṁ pattō sōūṇa tassimaṁ vayaṇaṁ ।
sō suttahāraputtō nivamittō pāyaḍō jāō ||627॥

sāhū mahavvayadharā, khamā guṇēṇaṁ khamā tullā ॥7॥
jaṁ jaha jiṇēhi bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ taha savvaṁ pamāṇamihavayaṇaṁ ।
iya saṁmattaṁ tattaṁ, pannattaṁ vīyarāgēhiṁ ॥8॥
jīvēhiṁ ēgachattaṁ rajjaṁ niravajjamahava dēvattaṁ ।
pattaṁ anaṁtasō vihu samattaṁ nēva saṁpattaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
jēhi vi muhuttamittaṁ sammattaṁ kaha vi phāsiyaṁ tāṇa ।
āsāyaṇabahulāṇa vi pariyaṭṭaddhaṁ bhavō hōhī ॥10 ॥
avi aviraipariṇāmā visuddhasammattamittamāhappā |
titthaṁkarāvi kē vi hu havaṁti kiṁ vannimō annaṁ ॥11॥
bhavabhamaṇamūlakāraṇamaṇaṁtasivasuhanivāraṇaṁ ghōraṁ ।
micchattaṁ titthayarā pariharaṇijjaṁ parūvaṁti ॥12॥
huṇaṇaṁ piṁḍapayāṇaṁ sōmaggahaṇāilōyakiccāī |
vajjē kuliṁgasaṁgaṁ lōiyatitthē tahāgamaṇaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
abbhāsavasēṇaṁ ciya pāyaṁ jīvāṇa hōi paḍivattī ।
ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ huṇaṇāī cayaṁti jattēṇa ॥14।।
ihalōyaparalōiyasuhāṇa savvāṇamāimanimittaṁ ।
sammattaṁ niravajjaṁ giṇhaha chaṁḍēha micchattaṁ ॥15॥
sammattaṁ pālitō niccalacittō ihēva jammammi ।
pāvai rajjaṁ purisō pannāyaramaṁti - puttō vva ॥ 16 ॥

-
kaṁcaṇamayapāyārā, maṇaharamaṇirayaṇa - nimmiyāgārā ।
atthi pasatthavihārā, sāvatthī nāma varanayarī ॥17॥
arināripattavallarisamūha - dhārāla - parasu - sāricchō ।

tassa ya gaiṁdagamaṇā miganayaṇā-chaṇa- sasaṁkasamavayaṇā ।

mayaṇaṁdōlaṇabhavaṇā dēvī rayaṇāvalī nāma ॥ 19 ॥
tāṇaṁ kālakamēṇaṁ puttō nīsēsadōsakulabhavaṇaṁ ।
jāō kūrō sīhō, sīhō nayahatthi saṁharēṇa ॥20॥
ittō ya buddhisāyaramaṁtisuō tassabālakālāō ।
pāruti mattō guṇamaṇirōhaṇagiri atthi ॥21॥
divvavasāphaṇimaṇiṇō pīyūsavisāṇi hariṇahariṇakā ।
jaha miliyā taha dunni vi viruddhasīlā vi tē miliyā ||22||
pattō ya maṁtiputtō nisīhasamayammi kaha vi jā niddaṁ ।
pariharai tāva picchai ujjāṇē maṇimaujjōyaṁ ॥23॥
kōūhalataralamaṇō jā gacchai tattha tā niyacchēi ।
taddiyahajāyanimmalavarakēvalanāṇa - saṁpannaṁ ॥24॥
nāmēṇa amiyatēyaṁ mahāmuṇiṁ hēmakamalasunisanaṁ ।
viyasiyamuhakamalēhiṁ sura asurēhiṁ mahijjaṁtaṁ ॥ 25 ॥ (juyalaṁ )
sō vi hu paṇāmapuvvaṁ uvaviṭṭhō tattha uciyadēsamma ।
bhayavaṁ pi kahai tattaṁ niruvamamahurāē vāṇīē ॥26॥
tahāhi-
saṁsārē nīrapūrē taraṇabharasahaṁ cārucammaṁ caritaṁ ।
saṁmattaṁ āyavattaṁ cauvihakaḍayāvāsiṇō bhavva lōyā ||
tēsiṁ mōhaṁdhayāraṁ kaliya jayagurū cakkavaṭṭī jiṇiṁdō ।
nāṇaṁ lōyappayāsaṁ maṇirayaṇanibhaṁ ṭhāvaē tattha sammaṁ ||27||
nāṇaṁ pi mōhatimiraṁ, harēi sammattasaṁjuyaṁ cēva ।
micchatta- mōhadōsā, taṁ pi hu vanaṁti appāṇaṁ ॥ 28 ॥
lavaṇāyarammi paḍiyaṁ jaha varavatthaṁ uvēi lavaṇattaṁ ।
micchattamajjha paḍiyaṁ taha nāṇaṁ havai micchattaṁ ॥29॥
tō chiṁdaha micchattaṁ, dharēha sammattasuddhapariṇāmaṁ ।
manēha jiṇābhihiyaṁ tattaṁ jai mahaha sivasōkkhaṁ ॥30॥

parapāsaṁḍipasaṁsā tēhi saha saṁthavō ya vicikicchā |
saṁkā kaṁkhā ya imē aiyārē casu sammattē ॥31 ॥
sōūṇa tassa vayaṇaṁ, maṁtisuō kēvalissa pāsamma |
paṁca aiyāramukkaṁ, sammattaṁ giṇhaē sammaṁ || 32॥
ittō ya rāyaputtō, navajuvvaṇaniviḍaṇatimirapasarēṇaṁ ।
uvahayavivēyanayaṇō, apahēsu payaṭṭaē niccaṁ ॥33॥
vasaṇāisatta sēvai duggaipatthāṇa maṁgalāṇi vva ।
jaṁ jaṁ picchai nayarē, rammaṁ avaharai taṁ savvaṁ ॥34॥
sō mittavayaṇamaṁkusamavagaṇiyamayagalu vva nayarammi ।
naravai āṇākhabhaṁ, ummūliya bhamai sacchaṁda ॥ 35॥
duvvilasiēṇa tassa ya mahāyaṇō divvavilasiēṇaṁ va ।
puṇṇarahiu vva savvō, nicca uvvēiō taiyā ॥36॥
samavāyaṁ kāūṇaṁ pavarajaṇō naravariṁdapāsamma ।
gaṁtuṁ vitravimaṇō, ciṭṭhai mōṇaṁ samallīṇō ||37||
tō nā saṁlattaṁ kiṁ ciṭṭhaha saṁpayaṁ pi bhīya vva ? ।
vinnavaha niyayakajjaṁ natthicchalaṁ ittha tumhāṇaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
tēsiṁ ēgō tattō, jaṁpai naranāha ! tujjha puttēṇaṁ ।
niyakulakittīē samaṁ nayarī savvā vi uddēviyā ॥ 39 ॥
jai tujha jahatthaṁ ciya sāhijjai tō havijja sō kumarō ।
amha viruddhō annaha, mayalijjai sāmi ! tuha vaṁsō ॥ 40 ॥

jō jaṇaviruddhakārī, sō sattū majjhana hu puttō ॥ 41 ॥
niyadēhasamuppannaṁ, lūyaviyāraṁ ca vivihaduhahēuṁ ।

kiṁ pi kahaṁ jēṇa suhaṁ gamijjaē ēttha paṁthammi ॥ 50 ॥
kalahaṁtā bhakkhatā bhayasaṁtatthā kahāṇaē laggā ।

iya taggirāya sahasā ghayasittō pāvaō vva sō jaliō ।
jaṁpai dhuttakaēṇaṁ dhiddhī naḍiōsi dhammēṇa ॥57॥
ghippai riughāēṇaṁ samuddapajjatamēiṇī rajjaṁ ।
pāvō ya sattaghāō tā rajjaṁ havaī pāvāō ॥58॥
visayasuhaṁ airammaṁ saṁpajjai vivihajīvaghāēṇaṁ ।
pāvō ya jīvaghāō tō niṁdasi mūḍha ! kiṁ pāvaṁ ॥ 59 ॥
iha tāva dhammiyāṇaṁ bhikkhā bhujjaṁ dharāē sayaṇijjaṁ ।
paralōē dhammēṇaṁ na yāṇimō tāṇa kiṁ hōhī ? ||60 ||
ēvaṁ vivayaṁtāṇaṁ mittāṇa vi tāṇa maccharō jāō ।
tē cēva buddhimaṁtā cayaṁti mittēṇa saha kalahaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
uktaṁ ca-
yadīcchēdvipulāṁ prītiṁ trīṇi tatra na kārayēt ।
vivādamarthasaṁraṁbha, parōkṣē dāradarśanam ॥62॥
tē pattā vivayaṁtā guṇagāmavivajjiyammi gāmammi |
pucchaṁti ya uvaviṭṭhaṁ parisāē gāmakuṁḍhajaṇaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
tō vayai rāyaputtō, jai maha vayaṇēṇa taṁ na bujjhēsi ।
tā puccha imaṁ lōyaṁ, dhammāhammāṇa māhappaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
tattō kaya- samavāyā, tēsiṁ sāhaṁti niyavisaṁvāyaṁ ।
dhammō ya ahammō vā, kō pavarō ittha bhavaṇammi ||65 ||
tō pāvasahāvēṇaṁ ahavā kumarassa pakkhavāēṇaṁ ।
jaṁpaṁti pāvamēvaya pasaṁsimō kaha vi nō dhammaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
vāṇijjaya- pasupālaṇa - kisīvalattāi - vivihapāvēhiṁ ।

ājammamaṁdhalā vi hu puṇana vā jāyaē diṭṭhī ॥ 108 ॥

hōhi tti jaṁpiūṇaṁ tirōhiyā jhatti vaṇadēvī ॥ 109 ॥
niyadaṁsaṇasaṁpuḍēṇaṁ nimmalanayaṇō tahiṁ jāō ॥ 110॥
uvvariyamōsahiṁ taṁ ghittuṁ maggammi vaccaē tattō ।
pattō ya hatthiṇāuragōuradārammi sō kamasō ॥ 111 ॥
tattha paḍahamuhēṇaṁ suṇēi āghōsaṇaṁ jahā ranō ।
jammaṁdhāē suyāē jō kō vi hu suddhajāi juō ॥ 112 ॥
ugghāḍai nayaṇajuyaṁ rāyā taṁ caiva kannayaṁ tassa ।
dāuṇa addharajjaṁ pasāyapuvvaṁ payacchēi ॥ 113 ॥
sō paḍahō bhamaḍaṁtō caukka - tiya- caccarāiṭhāṇēsu ।
bahuēhi vi divasēhiṁ puvvaṁ kēṇā vi na hu chittō ॥ 114 ॥
panāyaramaṁtisuō taddiṇapattō vi chivai taṁ paḍahaṁ ।
nīō ya rāyapāsē rāyāiṭṭhēhi purisēhiṁ ॥ 115 ॥
vinavai sō visāmi iya tuha kannaṁ sajjanayaṇasaṁpannaṁ ।
sajjaṁ karēmi jai maha uppāyisi paccayaṁ kamavi ॥ 116 ॥
vuḍḍhēṇamamaccēṇaṁ ēgēṇaṁ tassa savaṇamūlammi ।
saṇiyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ rāyā sō mayaraddhaō nāma ॥117॥
niravaccō niccaṁ pi hu puvviṁ pūēi vivihasuranivahaṁ ।
yacchai supattadāṇaṁ gacchai vēyālabhūmīsu ॥118॥

kaṁcaṇamālā nāmā kannā ēgā samuppannā ॥ 119॥

daṭṭhūṇa maṇuyalōyaṁ iha lukkai vihiya lajja vva ॥210॥
dīvatarammi gaṁtuṁ iha pattō kumara ! kiṁtu savvattha ।
hiḍaṁtēṇa vi na maē, ērisamaccubbhuyaṁ diṭṭha ॥211 ॥
sōūṇa imaṁ kumarō kōūhalataralamāṇasō dhaṇiyaṁ ।
puṇa purāviya vahaṇē caliō niyamittasaṁjuttō ॥ 212 ॥
paḍisiddhō vi hu ratnā kā daṁsaṇasamūsuō kamurō ।
na niyattō pattō uṇa jalanihimajjhammi divasēhiṁ ॥ 213 ॥
samayaṁtarammi diṭṭhā siriyā sirivacchalaṁchaṇēṇaṁ ca ।
sā niyayajaṇayabhavaṇē pattā lacchi vva paccakkhā ||214 ॥

picchaṁtī saviyāraṁ āyaḍhaṁti vva nibbuḍḍā ॥215॥
jaya tiyasaramaṇikulabhavaṇalavaṇajalarāsi nāsiya daridda ! |
sutthiyadēvāhiṭṭhiya dutthiyasāhāra dēsu piyaṁ ॥216॥
iya jaṁpirō kumārō vārijjatō niyayamittēṇa ।
karakaliya nisiyakhaggō, buḍḍhō tappiṭṭhaō sahasā ||217 ||

sayaṇāsaṇavasaṇāī kīliya pajjaṁtayaṁ lihiyaṁ ॥313 ॥
mucchā miliyacchi purā maṁ picchiya tē vayaṁti sacchaṁda ।
rē rē pucchaha ēyaṁ gihivara bhajjaṁ nihāṇāṇi ॥ 314॥
itthaṁtarammi dusahaduhakōḍikaḍakkhiyā mahā pāvā ।
divvōvahayā ahayaṁ sacēyaṇā takkhaṇā jāyā ||315॥
bhaṇiyā tēhiṁ nihāṇē kahēsu daṁsēsu niyaya pai jaṇaṇiṁ ।
tuma cciya niyalōō sahasā apavāhiō savva ॥ 316 ॥
paḍiuttaramakaritī jamabhaḍasarisēhiṁ tēhiṁ purisēhiṁ ।
maṁtissa samāēsā ēttha paēsē samāṇīyā ||317 ||
kiṁ ca-
paīmaraṇaṁ dhaṇanāsō taṇayābhāvō sudīharaṁ jīyaṁ ।
ēēhiṁ asaṁtuṭṭhō dhiṭṭhavihī dēu dharaṇaṁ pi ॥318॥
iccāi sappavaṁcaṁ pavaṁciuṁ sā vi dēvi payapuraō ।
hā nāha nāha ! bhaṇirī vilavaī uccēhiṁ saddēhiṁ ॥319॥
sōūṇa imaṁ dēvī ciṁtai ahahā nivāṇa nikkivayā ।
jē itthaṁ nivvīrādhaṇē vi lōhaṁ pakuvvaṁti ॥ 320 ॥
sukaṁ dāṇī daṁḍō, bhōgō bhāgō karō ya taha viṭṭhī ।
ēhiṁ asaṁtuṭṭhā, ahō nivāliṁti tīē dhaṇaṁ ॥321॥

rē ! muṁcasu maha dhūyaṁ nāsasu ahavā havēsu raṇasajjō ।
iya jaṁpatō pattō, vijjāharanāyagō tattha ॥ 416 ॥ juyalaṁ ॥
hā tāya ! rakkhiyāvāya, bhuvaṇatāyaṇaparāyaṇōvāya ! |
suṇiya niya jaṇayavayaṇā, iya kannā palavaē dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 417 ॥
vijjāharāṇa tāṇaṁ, avarupparamacchārāṇamacchēraṁ ।
picchaṁtāṇa kuṇatā, uttarapaccuttarā jāyā ॥ 418।।
tathāhi-
mā kō vi majjha duhiyaṁ, bhuvaṇāhivarūvasaṁpayākaliyaṁ ।
harihī avarō vi taō, imassa ranō samappissaṁ ॥ 419 ॥
iya jaṁpiūṇa bhaṇiō, kannā jaṇaēṇa sāyaraṁ rāyā ।
rakkhijjasu maha dhūyaṁ mā appasu avarapurisassa ॥420 ॥
jāva ahaṁ jiṇiūṇaṁ ēyaṁ duṭṭhaṁ samēmi tuha pāsē ।
tāva imaṁ maha dhūyaṁ, thavaṇīruvēṇa rakkhē ॥ 421 ॥
avarō vi khayararāyā, jaṁpai bhō rāya ! majjha varadaiyā ।
dhārēyavvā jāva ya ahayaṁ jujjhēmi ēēṇa ॥ 422॥
iya jaṁpirāṇa tāṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ vāyāē garuyasaṁgāmō |
saṁjāō abrunaṁ dūsaṇabhūsaṇavihāṇēhiṁ ॥423॥
muttūṇa visaṁvāyaṁ samavāyaṁ tē karitu tō rāyaṁ ।
pabhaṇaṁti tujjha kajjē samujjayā maccharucchaiyā ॥424॥

rē nikkāraṇavēriya ! hayavihi ! kiṁ tujjha kahasu avaraddhaṁ ? |

dhīrāṇamadāharaṇaṁ kiṁ hōuṁ kāyarō āsi ? ॥ 920॥
kiṁ dēva ! kō vi bhaviyavvayāē purisō surō va asurō vā ।
laliyaṁ parikaliyaṁ pi hu sakkō dūraṁ tu paḍiyārō ॥921 ॥
hu
purisā gavēsaṇatthaṁ taha vi nirūvē vividēsēsu ।
jai kō vi kaha vi suddhiṁ kattha vi lahihī gavēsaṁtō ॥922॥
rāyā tava kāuṁ caliō niyanayarasammuhaṁ kaha vi ।
jaṁ kajjaparicchēō taṁ ciya chēyāṇa chēyattaṁ ॥ 923 ॥
vicaliyavilakkhapuhaīsapamuhajaṇavayaṇamuṇiya suyaharaṇā ।
vilavēi tāratāraṁ jaṇaṇī kumarassa jayalacchī ॥924॥
hā lōuttamavācāhārahimasarisakittipabbhāra !
jiyamārasāravikkamakumāra ! hā kattha dīsihasi ? ॥ 925 ॥
paḍhamaṁ cēva na vaṁjjhā vihiyā kimiha hayāsa rē divva !
aha dinaṁ suyarayaṇaṁ hariyaṁ niddukkhatō kīsa ? ||926॥
annā vi savattīō saha tīē ruyaṁti kumaraharaṇammi ।

tāṇaṁ taṁ hi vayaṇaṁ, siṁhala - dīvammi divvajōēṇa ।
vaccissai jaṁ ahavā, saṁkai taṁ cēva pāvē ॥1223 ॥
tatthūjjāṇapaēsē, vihavaṁ vilasaṁtayāṇi sacchaṁdaṁ ।
dhammaṁ jhiyāyamāṇaṁ taṁ picchissaṁti muṇināhaṁ ॥। 1224 ||
kiṁ dēvayāē kiṁ vā, ēsō bhaviyavvayāē iha nayarē ।
mukku tti ciṁtayaṁtō, khāmissa taṁ sukaṁṭhō vi ॥ 1225 ।।

pēcchāmi taṁ na taṇumavi taṇummi tuha lakkhaṇaṁ kamavi ॥ 92 ॥
jēṇa tuha vaṁchiyatthō, ēsō saṁpajjaē asēsō vi ॥
dēvi jaṁpai dhuttō, sumarasu ēyaṁ niyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ।। 93 ।।
jai sayadiṇāṇa majjhē nāhaṁ sāhēmi bhāsiyaṁ niyayaṁ ॥
tā tuha paccakkhaṁ ciya, ciyāē pavisēmi kiṁ bahuṇā ? ॥ 94 ॥
aha nayarammi visaṁtō, puradārē niyai dāravāsiṇī bhavaṇaṁ ॥
citittu kimavi cittē, pavisai tatthēva bhavaṇammi ।। 95 ।।
kāūṇa karē khaḍiyaṁ, kaḍitta kattālayāimēlittā ||
,
jēvālakitavapamuhaṁ kappiya sō khillaē jūyaṁ ।। 96 ।।
laṁbōdarakhittāhika - jakkhāhiva - dāravāsiṇī - pamuhē ॥
chāhaṁ caḍāvayaṁtō, jiṇai imō ṭaṁkalakkhāṇi ॥ 97 ॥
saṁhariya aṁkaniyaraṁ, mahaṁtapāhāṇakhaṁḍakaliyakarō ॥
laṁbōdaraṁ payaṁpai, iṇhaṁ maha dēsu lahaṇijjaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
annaha tikōṇapāhaṇakōṇagghāēṇa laṁbamudaraṁ tē ।।
dārēmi ahaṁ ēsō, mā bhaṇihisi jaṁ na kahiyaṁti ॥ 99 ॥
iya jaṁpiya uppāḍai, taṁ uvalaṁ jāva tāva bhīēṇa ||
laṁbōdarēṇa dinnā, dō lakkhā tassa ṭaṁkāṇaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
ēvamavarē vi tiyasā gahiyā dhuttēṇa niya niyaṁ labdhaṁ ॥

gaṁtuṁ caṁpayamūlē, jhatti imō muttahāranivahēhiṁ ||

bhuvaṇāvayaṁsanayarē vimāṇajāṇēṇa pupphacūlō vi ॥
mōttūṇa tāṇa tinni vi sayaṁ niyaṁ ṭhāṇamaṇupattō ॥ 194 ।।
ēsō uṇa niuṇamaī, kumārapaḍibaṁdhabaddhamaṇavittī ॥
gihidhammaṁ kuvvaṁtō, nivasai tatthēva nayarammi ॥ 195 ।।
parivāliya gihidhammaṁ, dāṇaṁ dāūṇa samaṇasaṁghassa ॥
siddhataṁ lēhāviya, nimmāviya - biṁba- niuruṁbaṁ ॥ 196 ॥
uttaṁgasihararēhiramairammaṁ nimmavittu jiṇabhavaṇaṁ ॥
samaē vihiṇā tinni vi cayaṁti tē jajjaraṁ dēhaṁ ॥ 197 ॥
saṁkhō rayaṇavaī vi hu accuyakappammi niuṇabuddhīvi ॥
bāvīsasāgarāū, tinni vi tiyasā samuppannā ॥ 198 ॥
caviyā jaṁbuddīvē, ēkhaē pavaragōttajāīsu ॥
uvavannā kayapunnā, sāsaya- sōkkhaṁ lahissaṁti ॥ 199 ॥
jaha saṁkhakumārēṇaṁ, disiparimāṇaṁ na khaṁḍiyaṁ kaha vi ॥
taha na hi khaṁḍēyavvaṁ annēhi vi mōkkhakaṁkhīhiṁ ॥ 200 ॥
॥ iti digvatē śaṁkhakumārakathā samāptā ॥ gāthā 5228 ।।
bhōgōpabhōgaparimāṇavaē mahāpaumakumāra kahā :
disiparimāṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, inhi bhōgōva bhōgaparimāṇaṁ ॥
payaḍē saṁkhēvēṇaṁ, divaṁtajuyaṁ parūvēmi ॥ 201 ॥
bhujjaṁtamapuṇaruttaṁ, bhōgaṁ jāṇijja annakusumāī ||
puṇaruttaṁ bhujjaṁ bhajjā - sijjāiuvabhōgaṁ ॥ 202 ॥
bhōyaṇa - kamma vibhēyā, duvihaṁ bhōgōvabhōgaparimāṇaṁ ॥
mahu- makkhaṇāi - majjaṁ maṁsaṁ vajjijja paḍhamammi ॥ 203 ॥
paṁcuṁbari- annāyaṁ, phalaṁ ca vidalaṁ ca gōrasummīsaṁ ॥

sā caṁdalēhakannā, sasaṁbhamā bhaṇai taṁ ayāṇa vva ॥
jōiṇi sāmiṇi ! kō tē sīsō maha kahasu nibbhataṁ ॥ 693 ॥
dēvō vā asurō vā nāyakumārō vva kiṁnarō vā vi ॥
jō sīsō tujjha gōravvaṁ tassa kāyavvaṁ ॥ 694 ॥
sā jōiṇī payaṁpai sīsō na hu dēvajāiō kō vi ॥
kiṁ puṇa ēsō maṇuō, dullaliō nāma naranāhō ॥। 695 ॥
sā pabhaṇai avaṇāē, vēlaviyā taṁsi bhattilōhēṇa ॥
jaṁ bhaṇasi majjha puraō niyasīsaṁ maṇuyamittaṁ pi ॥ 696 ॥
tē jōiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ mayacchi ! mā bhaṇasu kiṁ pi iha atthē ॥
jaṁ maṁtapabhāvēṇaṁ, divvasarīrō kaō ēsō ॥ 697 ॥
tumaē vi au cēva ya ihāgaō jai vi taha vi iha nāō ||
jassa ahaṁ parituṭṭhā, kiṁ dulahaṁ tassa ti jaē vi ।। 698 ।।
tō divvasarīraṁ taṁ divvēṇa rasēṇa divvabhavaṇammi ||
taṁ divvasuṁdari ! sayaṁ jēmāvasu majjha vayaṇēṇa ॥ 699 ।।
tujjha pamāṇaṁ vayaṇaṁ ti jaṁpiūṇaṁ imā vi taṁ thālaṁ ॥'
uccariya bhattapunnaṁ uppāḍai niyaya hatthēṇa ॥ 700 ॥

jaha sā kannā hatthī, jaṇō vi niddāi asēsō vi ॥

niddā vigamē kannā, harisavisāē maṇammi samakālaṁ ॥.
uvvahamāṇā kaṁṭhē varamālaṁ khivai kumarassa ॥ 991 ॥
haricaṁda amaccēhiṁ, vikkamasēṇēṇa taha ya duṇhaṁ pi ॥
tēsiṁ vīvāhamahō, vihiṇā vihiō vibhūīē ॥ 992 ॥
vihiē dasāhiyamahē, caliō gahiūṇa rāyavarakannaṁ ॥
kamasō ya paṭṭaṇaṁ, paṭṭaṇamēsā samaṇupattō ॥ 993 ॥

taṁ jhatti cittasālaṁ, sajjaṁtī picchiūṇa sē bhajjā |
saddāviūṇa sāhai taṁ savvaṁ niyaya nāhassa ॥ 1185 ॥
,
pāvāṇa ya punnāṇa ya, vilasiyamēyaṁ imassa dhuvamēyaṁ ॥
citittu tēṇa bhajjā, nivāriyā kahasu mā kassa ॥ 1186 ॥
bhuttuttarammi ēsō, dhaṇasēṇēṇaṁ payaṁpiō majjha ||
bhāyāsi taō tujjha vi, akahittā tammi diyahammi ॥ 1187 ॥
maṇimālā saṁgahiyā, maē tō tīē asamamāhappā ॥
ittiyamittō savvō, samajjiō vihavavitthārō ॥ 1188 ॥
niyamaṇimālaṁ ēyaṁ tattō giṇhēsu jaṁpiuṁ ēvaṁ ||
sā maṇimālā tēṇaṁ, samappiyā tassa vaṇiyassa ।। 1189 ।।
sō ciṁtai piccha ahō, māhappamimassa purisarayaṇassa ॥
saṁpai maha bhajjāē, saccaviyā sā vi muccaṁtī ॥ 1190 ॥
taiyā imēṇa diṭṭhā, gilijjamāṇā ya taha ya navi ēsō ॥
niya mahimāē asaṁbhavivatthaṁ parijaṁpara kahavi ॥ 1191 ।।
niya acchipicchiyaṁ pi hu paṭṭamasamaṁ samīhamāṇēhiṁ ||
nēva asaddahaṇijjaṁ, kahaṇijjaṁ garuyapurisēhiṁ ॥ 1192 ॥
uktaṁ ca :-
aśraddhēyaṁ na vaktavyaṁ, pratyakṣaṁ yadi dr̥śyatē ॥
tathā vānarasaṁgītaṁ, tathā tarati sā śilā ।। 1193 ॥
,
iya niyamēṇa vibhāviya, sō pabhaṇai bhāuṇō vi niyayassa ॥
kiṁ kuṇasi vippayāraṇamasaccamēyaṁ payaṁpaṁtō ॥ 1194 ॥
ijjāi jaṁpiūṇaṁ, sudaṁsaṇēṇaṁ imassa savvō vi ॥
niya bhajjā saccaviō, vr̥ttaṁtō sāhiō sammaṁ ॥ 1195 ॥
dhaṇasēō vi hu savvaṁ, jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva tassa kahiūṇaṁ ॥

gaṁtūṇaṁ sūranāhā, māṇavathaṁbhassa uvarimmi ॥ 1375 ॥
vajjasamuggayamajjhē, muyaṁti pūyaṁti tāu dāḍhāō ||
tēsiṁ thūyāē maṁgalavijayā sayā hōṁti । 1376 ॥
siri sumaijiṇē mukkhaṁ paramappahō sivaṁ pattō ॥
nauīē sahassēsuṁ gaēsu ayarāṇakōḍīṇaṁ ॥ 1377 ॥
ēvaṁ vakkaṁtāsuṁ bahusu aiyarōvamāṇakōḍīsu ॥
siddhattharāyaputtō upannō vīrajiṇanāhō । 1378 ।।
sirivaddhamāṇatitthē jaṁbū pabhavāimuṇigaṇidēsu ||
suṭṭhiyasuppaḍibuddhō, gaēsu sūrī samuppanna || 1379 ।।

ēyāsi pasāhōṇaṁ, kō jāṇai savva nāmāṇi ॥ 1382 ।।
vijjāharasāhāē, gacchā guccha vva sumaṇamaṇaharaṇā ||
jāliharakā saharayā, muṇimahuyaraparigayā dōnni || 1383 ॥

ahamahamigāē bahavē, piyaṁti siddhaṁtasirināhaṁ ।। 1384 ॥
tattha ya :-
jāō tārai sairēhiratalē, gacchammi vōmaṁgaṇē,
dhammajjhāṇamaṇīnihāṇakalasō sōbālacaṁdō muṇī ॥
appaṁ kammamalīmasaṁ paḍidiṇaṁ sōhaṁtaō jō sayā,
ahiṁ uvāsahiṁ amalaṁ tēvē tavaṁ duttavaṁ ॥ 1385 ।।
sīsā tassa jayaṁtu sakkasarisā mōhaṁ mahāpavvayaṁ,
tikkhēṇaṁ caraṇēṇa thōrapaviṇā cuṇṇaṁ kuṇaṁtā sayā ।।
lōyāṇaṁ guṇabhaddasūriguruṇō sārassayaṁ savvayā,

siṁ paṭṭiyōnihimmi kamalā baṁdhūmaṇī nimmalō,
savvāṇaṁdaguru asēsajagaī jaṁghālakittībharō ||
jaṁ kāuṁ hiyaēkkaladdhavasahi saṁtō samaṁtāsirī,
pabbhāraṁ purisōttamattamahuṇā kē kē na pattā sayā ॥ 1387 ।।
vayaṇāu jassa niggayamaṇēyavibuhāṇa vihiyamaṇi harisaṁ ॥
amayaṁ va sāyarāō, cariyaṁ siripāsasāmissa ॥ 1388 ॥

rēṇukkarēṇu ṇhāyā, jalaṁjali jattha dēṁti dukkhāṇaṁ ॥

siripaumappahasāmicariyaṁ
vēyasarasūra paramiya [1254] varisē nivavikkamassa varisāō ॥
maggasirasuddhadasamī, tihīi vārammi taha raviṇō ॥ 1392 ॥
rēvai nakkhattagaē himakiraṇē vēribhīmabhīmassa ||
cālukkavaṁsamuṇiṇō, niravajjē rajjasamayammi ॥ 1393 ।।
sirivaddhamāṇanayarē, ṭhiēṇa pajjūnnasēṭṭhivasahīē ॥
siripaumappahacariyaṁ, paḍiputramiṇaṁ maē vihiyaṁ ।। 1394 ।।
samaṇōvāsagaviddayalakkhaṇaabbhatthaṇā ihaṁ ||
>
paḍhamaṁ jāyā majjha pavittī, paumappahacariyanimmāṇē ।। 1395 ॥
jaṁ siddhaṁtaviruddhaṁ, lakkhaṇahīṇaṁ ca jaṁpiyaṁ ēttha ॥
taṁ khamau majjha savvaṁ, suyaṁ ca suyadhāriṇō cēva ॥ 1396 ॥
jai vi nava kavvavisayā sattī maha nēva samayajalanihiṇō ||
paramaṁ pārīṇattaṁ chēyattaṁ nēva uttī ।। 1397 ॥
tahavi bhaē asamāē. paumappahatitthamahimāē ||
pāraddhamiṇaṁ cariyaṁ, nivigdhaṁ taha ya sammattaṁ ॥ 1398 ॥
karttuṁ na prakaṭayaṁ sphurannava nava prauḍhārthadr̥ṣṭiṁ mayā
tō tatvāni nivēṣṭumatra bhagavatsiddhāntasiddhāni vā ॥
naiva khyāpayituṁ vyadhāyi, caritaṁ rītiṁ vidarbhōdbhavāṁ
bhaktiṁ kintu punaḥ puna rna gaditaṁ śrī padmalakṣmaprabhōḥ ।। 1399 ।।
ummīlati niraṁtaramatthā saddā ya jaṁ navā majjhē ॥
tē dēviṁdaguruṇaṁ pasāyamahimāi maha mahiyaṁ || 1400 ॥
tarkānadhītya dēvēndragurōḥ siddhāntamāditaḥ ||
śrī haribhadrasūribhyaścaritaṁ nirmamē mayā । 1401 ॥
aṁcai sāsayatitthē nahalacchī jāva rikkhakusumēhiṁ ॥
sasi - ravivaratāḍaṁkā naṁdau cariyaṁ imaṁ tāva ।। 1402 ॥
jāliharagacchanahayalamayaṁkasiridēvasūriraiyammi ||
siri paumappahacariē saṁmattō turiyapatthāvō || 1403 ॥

gaṁthakāra satthi
॥ iti śrīmatpadmaprabhacaritaṁ samāptaṁ ॥ chaḥ || gāthā 7232 ॥
kr̥tiriyaṁ śrī jāliharagacchamaṁḍana śrīdharmmaghōṣa-
sūri śiṣya śrī dēvasūriṇāmiti bhadraṁ । śrīḥ || chaḥ ॥
āśirvādō'yaṁ saṁghasya likhyatē yathā :-
kāryāṇāmaniśaṁ yataḥ śivakarī siddhiṁ samāsādyatē,
yasmātsarvamanōrathadrumatatirviśvasya paṁphulyatē
anyadyacca manōrathātigamahō sarvaṁ samāsādyatē
yuṣmākaṁ bhavatācchubhāśayavatāṁ padmaprabhaḥ saśriyē ॥ 1404 ॥
ēlā yatra dayā kṣamā ca lavatī satyaṁ lavaṁgaṁ paraṁ,
kāruṇyaṁ kramukī, phalāni viditaścarṇaśca satvōdayaḥ ||
karpūraṁ munidānamuttamaguṇaṁ śīlaṁ ca patrōccayā,
gr̥hnīdhvaṁ guṇakr̥jjanairnigaditaṁ tāṁbūlamētajjanāḥ || 1405 ।।
